id=\"first_ch_divider\"> \n\n<h4 style=\"display: none;\">By <a href=\"http://operationrainfall.com/author/dmannlives/\" title=\"Posts by Dalton McClain\" rel=\"author\">Dalton McClain</a> <small class=\"postmetadata\"><b> / </b> April 20th, 2017 </small>\n\n<i class=\"fa fa-toggle-off toggle-light\"></i>\n<i class=\"fa fa-toggle-on\"></i>\n</h4>\n\n<hr id=\"ch_divider\"> \n\n\t</div>\n\n\t  \t<p><img data-attachment-id=\"232775\" data-permalink=\"http://operationrainfall.com/2017/04/04/opinion-persona-5s-video-restrictions-puts-a-ball-and-chain-on-content-creators/t_persona5_teaser/\" data-orig-file=\"https://i2.wp.com/operationrainfall.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/t_persona5_teaser.jpg?fit=1280%2C720\" data-orig-size=\"1280,720\" data-comments-opened=\"1\" data-image-meta=\"{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}\" data-image-title=\"Persona 5 | Ball and Chain\" data-image-description=\"\" data-medium-file=\"https://i2.wp.com/operationrainfall.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/t_persona5_teaser.jpg?fit=300%2C169\" data-large-file=\"https://i2.wp.com/operationrainfall.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/t_persona5_teaser.jpg?fit=610%2C343\" class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-232775\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/operationrainfall.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/t_persona5_teaser.jpg?resize=610%2C343\" alt=\"Persona 5 | Ball and Chain\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/operationrainfall.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/t_persona5_teaser.jpg?resize=610%2C343 610w, https://i2.wp.com/operationrainfall.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/t_persona5_teaser.jpg?resize=195%2C110 195w, https://i2.wp.com/operationrainfall.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/t_persona5_teaser.jpg?resize=300%2C169 300w, https://i2.wp.com/operationrainfall.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/t_persona5_teaser.jpg?resize=768%2C432 768w, https://i2.wp.com/operationrainfall.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/t_persona5_teaser.jpg?w=1280 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 610px) 100vw, 610px\" width=\"418\" height=\"235\"></p>\n<p>Recently, it’s come to light that Atlus has registered a wide variety of <em>Persona</em> domains. These include&nbsp;P3D, P5AG, P5D, P5R, P5U, Persona Dance, and PQ2. They’ve also registered every <em>Persona</em> name up to 10, so that’s also very promising. This is exciting news to fans of the series, as this means we’re getting a lot more spinoff games to tie us over until we get <em>Persona 6</em> in about 10 years.</p>\n<p>I have some theories as to what these games might be, but we’ll just have to wait for more news to come out. What do you think? Tell us your ideas and theories in the comments down below.</p>\n<ul>\n<li>P3D –<em> Persona 3 Dancing</em></li>\n<li>P5AG – Like <em>Persona 4 Golden</em>, an enhanced version.</li>\n<li>P5D – <em>Persona 5 Dancing</em></li>\n<li>P5R – <em>Persona 5 Racing</em></li>\n<li>P5U – A new arena fighting game.</li>\n<li>Persona Dance – A dancing game based around either the first <em>Persona</em> game, or all of them combined.</li>\n<li>PQ2 – <em>Persona Q 2</em></li>\n</ul>\n<twitterwidget class=\"twitter-tweet twitter-tweet-rendered\" id=\"twitter-widget-0\" data-tweet-id=\"855005856882204673\" style=\"position: static; visibility: visible; display: block; transform: rotate(0deg); max-width: 100%; width: 500px; min-width: 220px; margin-top: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;\"></twitterwidget>\n<p><script async=\"\" src=\"//platform.twitter.com/widgets.js\" charset=\"utf-8\"></script></p>\n<footer class=\"author_bio_section row well\"><p class=\"author_name lead\">About Dalton McClain</p><p class=\"author_details lead\"><img alt=\"\" src=\"http://2.gravatar.com/avatar/e5d164c4235fd596bb58f7d2d9916919?s=90&amp;d=retro&amp;r=r\" srcset=\"http://2.gravatar.com/avatar/e5d164c4235fd596bb58f7d2d9916919?s=180&amp;d=retro&amp;r=r 2x\" class=\"avatar avatar-90 photo grav-hashed grav-hijack\" height=\"90\" width=\"90\" id=\"grav-e5d164c4235fd596bb58f7d2d9916919-0\">A gamer at heart, and a creator by trade. As a shy kid who grew up in a small town, my only solace was with the games that I enjoyed playing. That being said I enjoy just about every type of game, but more than anything I love playing horror/unique games. I look forward to sharing my knowledge of the strange and unusual with the world.</p><p class=\"author_links\"><a href=\"http://operationrainfall.com/author/dmannlives/\">View all posts by Dalton
